  }

  &.size-xs {

    min-width: 3.5rem;

    border-radius: 0.25rem;
    font-size: 0.75rem;
    gap: 0.25rem;
  }

  }

    box-shadow: var(--tw-ring-offset-shadow), var(--tw-ring-shadow);
  }

  /* Primary variant */
  &.primary {

      0 1px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05);
    text-shadow: 0 1px 2px rgb(0 0 0 / 10%);

    &:hover {
      background-position: 100% 0%;
      background-image: linear-gradient(
        to right,
        hsl(var(--accent-main-200)) 0%,
        hsl(var(--accent-main-200)) 100%

    }

    &:hover {
      background-color: hsl(var(--accent-main-200));

24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Authentication methods</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Setting up Claude Code requires access to Anthropic models. For teams, you can set up Claude Code access in one of these ways:</span>
<ul>
<li><a href="#claude-for-teams-or-enterprise" class="link">Claude for Teams or Enterprise</a> (recommended)</li>
<li><a href="#claude-console-authentication" class="link">Claude Console</a></li>
<li><a class="link" href="/docs/en/amazon-bedrock">Amazon Bedrock</a></li>
<li><a class="link" href="/docs/en/google-vertex-ai">Google Vertex AI</a></li>
<li><a class="link" href="/docs/en/microsoft-foundry">Microsoft Foundry</a></li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="claude-for-teams-or-enterprise"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#claude-for-teams-or-enterprise" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Claude for Teams or Enterprise</span></h3>
<span data-as="p"><a href="https://claude.com/pricing#team-&amp;-enterprise" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Claude for Teams</a> and <a href="https://anthropic.com/contact-sales" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Claude for Enterprise</a> provide the best experience for organizations using Claude Code. Team members get access to both Claude Code and Claude on the web with centralized billing and team management.</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Claude for Teams</strong>: self-service plan with collaboration features, admin tools, and billing management. Best for smaller teams.</li>
<li><strong>Claude for Enterprise</strong>: adds SSO, domain capture, role-based permissions, compliance API, and managed policy settings for organization-wide Claude Code configurations. Best for larger organizations with security and compliance requirements.</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="claude-console-authentication"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#claude-console-authentication" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Claude Console authentication</span></h3>

contentEditable="false" data-component-part="step-title">Install Claude Code</p><div data-component-part="step-content" class="prose dark:prose-invert"><span data-as="p">Users can <a class="link" href="/docs/en/setup#installation">install Claude Code</a>.</span></div></div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="credential-management"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#credential-management" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Credential management</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Claude Code securely manages your authentication credentials:</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Storage location</strong>: on macOS, API keys, OAuth tokens, and other credentials are stored in the encrypted macOS Keychain.</li>
<li><strong>Supported authentication types</strong>: Claude.ai credentials, Claude API credentials, Azure Auth, Bedrock Auth, and Vertex Auth.</li>
<li><strong>Custom credential scripts</strong>: the <a class="link" href="/docs/en/settings#available-settings"><code>apiKeyHelper</code></a> setting can be configured to run a shell script that returns an API key.</li>
<li><strong>Refresh intervals</strong>: by default, <code>apiKeyHelper</code> is called after 5 minutes or on HTTP 401 response. Set <code>CLAUDE_CODE_API_KEY_HELPER_TTL_MS</code> environment variable for custom refresh intervals.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="see-also"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#see-also" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">â€‹<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">See also</span></h2>

message);\n}\n\nfunction shouldIgnore(name) {\n  const ignoreList = [\n    \".git\",\n    \".gitignore\",\n    \"node_modules\",\n    \"mint.json\",\n    \"deploy.sh\",\n    \"package.json\",\n    \"package-lock.json\",\n    \"CODEOWNERS\",\n    \"CLAUDE.md\",\n    \"ruff.toml\",\n    \"tox.ini\",\n    \"script.js\",\n    \".DS_Store\",\n    \".pytest_cache\",\n    \"__pycache__\",\n  ];\n\n = fs.readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });\n    for (const entry of entries) {\n      const fullPath = path.join(dir, entry.name);\n      if (entry.isDirectory()) {\n        files.push(...findMdxFiles(fullPath));\n      } else if (entry.name.endsWith(\".mdx\")) {\n        files.push(fullPath);\n      }\n    }\n    return files;\n  };\n\n  const mdxFiles = copyImages() {\n  log(\"\\n\" + \"=\".repeat(60));\n  log(\"Copying images...\");\n  log(\"=\".repeat(60) + \"\\n\");\n\n  const imagesSrc = path.join(DOCS_REPO_DIR, \"images\");\n  const imagesDest = ${imagePath}`);\n    } else {\n      log(`  âš  Image not found: ${imagePath}`);\n    }\n  }\n\n  log(`\\nâœ“ Copied ${imageCount} referenced images (out of ${referencedImages.length} Generate filtered docs.json with only Claude Code content\n */\nfunction generateDocsJson() {\n  log(\"\\n\" + \"=\".repeat(60));\n  log(\"Generating filtered docs.json...\");\n  log(\"=\".repeat(60) const filteredNavigation = {\n    languages: [],\n  };\n\n  docsData.navigation.languages.forEach((langVersion) =\u003e {\n    const languageCode = langVersion.language;\n\n    // Find Claude Code tab\n    const claudeCodeTab = langVersion.tabs.find((tab) =\u003e tab.tab === \"Claude Code\");\n\n    if (!claudeCodeTab) {\n      log(`  - No Claude Code tab found for language: ${languageCode}`);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Find Admin API tab and filter to only Claude Code endpoints\n    let adminApiClaudeCodeGroup = null;\n    const adminApiTab = langVersion.tabs.find((tab) =\u003e tab.tab === \"Admin API\");\n\n    if (adminApiTab) {\n      // Find the Claude Code group within Admin API\n      const findClaudeCodeGroup = (groups) =\u003e {\n        for (const group of groups) {\n          if (group.group === \"Claude Code\") {\n            return group;\n          }\n          if (group.pages) {\n            for (const page of group.pages)   {\n              group: group.group,\n              pages: group.pages || [],\n            },\n          ],\n        });\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Add Admin API tab if Claude Code endpoints ${languageCode} (${tabs.length} tabs)`);\n  });\n\n  // Create new docs.json with filtered content\n  const filteredDocsJson = {\n    ...docsData,\n    name: \"Claude Code Docs\",\n    navigation: function updatePaths(obj) {\n    if (typeof obj === 'string') {\n      // Replace /docs/claude-code/ with / for all language codes\n      let updated = obj.replace(/(^|\\/)((en|fr|de|it|ja|es|ko|zh-CN|zh-TW|ru|id|pt))\\/docs\\/claude-code\\//g, '$1$2/');\n      // Also replace /claude-code/ with / for all language codes (for paths that don't have updatePaths(value);\n      }\n      return updated;\n    }\n    return obj;\n  }\n\n  // Update all paths in the docs.json to reflect the flattened structure\n  const updatedDocsJson = */\nfunction findReferencedSnippets() {\n  const referencedSnippets = new Set();\n\n  // Find all MDX files we just copied\n  const findMdxFiles = (dir) =\u003e {\n    const files = [];\n    if
